They have been consistently great, we have been using them for mini-leases for years. They always take care to give you the best vehicle they have and we've had no problems with exchanging them when anything mechanical has come up through normal wear and tear. The staff at this branch in particular seem to know the system very well and will give you a much more personal service than you might expect from a busy airport desk.

Only downside compared to a bigger branch at an airport is that the vehicle selection can be limited on busy days, but I'll still use them in preference if at all possible.</text>

Expensive paint that's worth it.
I like the folks that work here. No nonsense and very helpful. Having troubles choosing colors? Hire their colorist. The colorist will even make house calls to work out all the details and help to coordinate your color scheme. We'll worth the $90 to have someone help us in deciding home colors. The paint here is the bomb. Long lasting with easy application and cleanup (latex, air sprayer/brush). Try to buy during sale periods to save a buck. $66 per gallon can be had for $50 during the right time. Even then, $66 is worth it if you're only having to paint every 20 years.</text>

<userid>116104991481152235335</userid><user_name>Jasmine Jan</user_name><Date>1602676167724< /Date><rating>5</rating>< text>
I began accepting credit/debit/HSA/FSA card payments in my outpatient psychiatric practice with the onset of the COVID pandemic. I did a lot of research and learned that the merchants who charge a flat monthly fee are more cost effective and Merchant Processing Group's was the lowest I could find. They had an extensive security vetting process, which was comforting, and the few initial hiccups that I encountered were easily fixed because I was readily able to get someone on the phone in a reasonable amount of time. The onboarding, once past the security clearance, was easy and the Virtual Terminal is ridiculously easy to use and makes me think I may not need to actual hardware Bluetooth terminal offered for in office use once I begin seeing patients in my office again. Once the pandemic is passed, I will maintain the relationship with Merchant Processing Group.< /text>

<user_name>Gizofi Leand</user_name><Date>1602673748872< /Date><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
Finding a good and honest merchant service provider (MSP) is very difficult nowadays. In the past three years, we've had to leave three MSPs because of dishonest fees or batch failures (basically, this is when a merchant doesn't receive funds earned in their bank account). We have now been with Merchant Processing Group for about three months and I'm happy to say that -- so far -- there have been no unpleasant billing surprises. Merchant Processing Group is honest and upfront with their fees. There was one technical error where we didn't receive the full amount of funds earned, but Merchant Processing Group's friendly support staff resolved the issue within 24 hours (other MSPs could take up to one week to resolve processor errors). Small businesses looking for a good and honest MSP should seriously consider Merchant Processing Group.</text>

I adore this place. This is where I pay my tithes, because of the excellent service and knowledge that is gifted into my life with each visit. There are many shades, if you will, to this space; all moving toward total body health & clarity of mind & of space. <date>1516293709019</date><rate>1< /rate>< Review>
DO NOT let the new pretty decorations they're working on fool you. This place is the worst kind of nightmare. Especially stay away from Michael--from my experience with him and the other reviews I've read about him, he's a bit of a monster. But The Grand doesn't care about tenant satisfaction, they care about their bottom line, so it's likely he'll remain there.

Alright, let's break this all down.

1. We toured in Jan 2017 with Anthony and he told us there'd be construction and installation of washers/dryers into each unit, but promised ours wouldn't be touched until we moved out. Bold face lie--they started a "3 week" construction project in our unit that lasted well into November because they screwed up and had to start over. Rent would not be lowered and anyone who refused was evicted.

2. Because of all the construction throughout the entire building, one of my roommates stepped on a rusty nail in one of the stairwells leading outside. We sent two emails, one of them being directly to the project manager, Justin. Neither were responded to and no action was taken. Not even an apology.

3. There seemed to be a discrepancy with our move-out agreement, as we received a bill in the mail for rent through the end of January despite having already officially moved out January 3rd and our move-out agreement being signed and submitted in time. I was told to disregard that bill after calling them out on it, but I'm in disbelief that it was sent in the first place.

4. Speaking of billing issues! We couldn't pay one of our rent payments on time because they did not bill us for that month. They hit us with a late fee for that despite it not at all being our fault, and they would not just eat that cost themselves without getting something out of it for them (despite it, again, being their fault). So Michael said he'd only do that if we wrote a positive Yelp review. He extorted a positive Yelp review out of us so we didn't have to pay a late fee that was in no way our fault. We have since updated that review to reflect a more accurate portrayal of how our experience at The Grand went.

5. Water was constantly being shut off, fire alarms would blare all the time and in the wee hours of the morning, the credit card machines in the laundry rooms were constantly broken, elevators were regularly broken or out of commission for "maintenance," the pool and exercise room were closed for a majority of the time we lived there. We even found dog feces in the hallways on more than one occasion.

6. Now, at the end of it all, I signed a paper with a quote for what our move-out costs would be. It's almost hysterical how different those costs ended up being. They quoted me $75 to touch up the paint. They charged us $265. When I brought it up to them over the phone, Michael tried to argue with me. He said that since one of the other costs was quoted at $120 and ended up being $16, I should be fine with it! Because it evens out!

No, Michael, the fact that our general cleaning cost went down from $120 to $16 does not in any way make up for or "even out" the difference from the $75 for painting I was quoted to $265 we were actually charged. Nevermind that the numbers don't even out at all (still close to $100 not being "made up" for there), the fact that we were quoted one thing and were met with a VERY drastic change is completely unacceptable. Valiant effort though! But maybe don't take such a snippy tone with me next time?

Everyone you encounter at The Grand will lie to you. From the very start, before we even signed a single paper, we were lied to by Anthony. We were lied to by Justin about the status of the construction project. We were lied to about our move-out costs. All every one of them does is lie.

The Grand clearly has a very severe customer service and management issue. I assume no one cares about that so long as they get their paycheck so c'est la vie. Hopefully people reading these reviews will heed all of our warnings and stay as many miles away from this place as possible.</Review>
